<review>Love that Lady M Cake Boutique is conveniently located inside Santa Anita Mall.

We decided to pick up a few cakes from here to celebrate Lunar New Year and my dad's birthday. We chose the matcha and the seasonal red bean mille crepe cakes.

The presentation at Lady M is simple, clean and elegant. We love the simplicity of their cakes and the depth of the flavors. You can buy whole cakes and slices. If you are going to buy whole cakes, make sure you go earlier during the day as they run out fast.

My all-time favorite mille crepe cake is the matcha. It's full of matcha flavor, slightly sweet that complements the matcha flavor. The top of the cake is dusted with more matcha powder. If you are a big matcha lover like me, this is the cake you will want to get.

The seasonal red bean mille crepe cake had the cream from their original mille crepe cake along with red bean paste and red bean.

Keep in mind that the prices of cakes tend to be on the high side, Lady M Cake Boutique is definitely a splurge.< /review>< rating>

<rating>4</rating>< Review>
Chengdu style hotpot in LA!  Quick guide:  I recommend the combo half and half bone broth/medium to hot spicy soup to cook in.  Order the combo meat (beef and lamb), fresh beef, winter melon, daikon, vegetable combo, quail eggs. Create dipping sauce: 1 teaspoon soy sauce, heaps of fresh garlic, green onion, and a slash of vinegar. Cook items and dip b4 eating.  Drink: watermelon juice or Sapporo.</Review>

<Text>This was my first real hot pot experience and it was incredible! It helped tremendously that my date is originally from Taiwan and speaks Chinese fluently (I saw on the roster that there were 23 parties ahead of us, but he spoke to the hostess and she took us right in- score!). We ordered a plethora of vegetables including: Daikon radish, Chinese cabbage, lotus root, enoki mushrooms, mung beans and others, as well as both mushroom broth and spicy broth plus lamb, spicy beef and original flavor and a type of small bony fish.

We retrieved our own sauce mixes from a small buffet type of setup where desserts and other appetizers were available too. I had never experienced this unique and bizarre response in my palate before- the Sichuan pepper. Wow! Talk about an exciting aspect to the meal. If you masticate the peppers, they cause a tingling and numbing sensation in your mouth. It paired really pleasantly with the pepper beef we ordered, but interestingly enough altered the flavors of other things I consumed. They had three types of sesame balls, one being my favorite- red bean with glutinous rice. I loved it. I can't wait to return for more hot pot options!<//Text>< gmap_id>
